</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，函数f的最后一步是调用函数g，这就叫尾调用。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">以下三种情况，都不属于尾调用。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">// 情况一
function f(x){
  let y = g(x);
  return y;
}

// 情况二
function f(x){
  return g(x) + 1;
}

// 情况三
function f(x){
  g(x);
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，情况一是调用函数g之后，还有赋值操作，所以不属于尾调用，即使语义完全一样。情况二也属于调用后还有操作，即使写在一行内。情况三等同于下面的代码。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function f(x){
  g(x);
  return undefined;
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">尾调用不一定出现在函数尾部，只要是最后一步操作即可。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function f(x) {
  if (x &gt; 0) {
    return m(x)
  }
  return n(x);
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，函数m和n都属于尾调用，因为它们都是函数f的最后一步操作。</p><h3 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">尾调用优化</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">尾调用之所以与其他调用不同，就在于它的特殊的调用位置。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">我们知道，函数调用会在内存形成一个“调用记录”，又称“调用帧”（call frame），保存调用位置和内部变量等信息。如果在函数A的内部调用函数B，那么在A的调用帧上方，还会形成一个B的调用帧。等到B运行结束，将结果返回到A，B的调用帧才会消失。如果函数B内部还调用函数C，那就还有一个C的调用帧，以此类推。所有的调用帧，就形成一个“调用栈”（call stack）。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">尾调用由于是函数的最后一步操作，所以不需要保留外层函数的调用帧，因为调用位置、内部变量等信息都不会再用到了，只要直接用内层函数的调用帧，取代外层函数的调用帧就可以了。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function f() {
  let m = 1;
  let n = 2;
  return g(m + n);
}
f();

// 等同于
function f() {
  return g(3);
}
f();

// 等同于
g(3);
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，如果函数g不是尾调用，函数f就需要保存内部变量m和n的值、g的调用位置等信息。但由于调用g之后，函数f就结束了，所以执行到最后一步，完全可以删除 f(x) 的调用帧，只保留 g(3) 的调用帧。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">这就叫做“尾调用优化”（Tail call optimization），即只保留内层函数的调用帧。如果所有函数都是尾调用，那么完全可以做到每次执行时，调用帧只有一项，这将大大节省内存。这就是“尾调用优化”的意义。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">注意，只有不再用到外层函数的内部变量，内层函数的调用帧才会取代外层函数的调用帧，否则就无法进行“尾调用优化”。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function addOne(a){
  var one = 1;
  function inner(b){
    return b + one;
  }
  return inner(a);
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面的函数不会进行尾调用优化，因为内层函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">inner</code>用到了外层函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">addOne</code>的内部变量<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">one</code>。</p><h3 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">尾递归</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">函数调用自身，称为递归。如果尾调用自身，就称为尾递归。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">递归非常耗费内存，因为需要同时保存成千上百个调用帧，很容易发生“栈溢出”错误（stack overflow）。但对于尾递归来说，由于只存在一个调用帧，所以永远不会发生“栈溢出”错误。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function factorial(n) {
  if (n === 1) return 1;
  return n * factorial(n - 1);
}

factorial(5) // 120
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码是一个阶乘函数，计算n的阶乘，最多需要保存n个调用记录，复杂度 O(n) 。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果改写成尾递归，只保留一个调用记录，复杂度 O(1) 。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function factorial(n, total) {
  if (n === 1) return total;
  return factorial(n - 1, n * total);
}

factorial(5, 1) // 120
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">还有一个比较著名的例子，就是计算fibonacci 数列，也能充分说明尾递归优化的重要性</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果是非尾递归的fibonacci 递归方法</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function Fibonacci (n) {
  if ( n &lt;= 1 ) {return 1};

  return Fibonacci(n - 1) + Fibonacci(n - 2);
}

Fibonacci(10); // 89
// Fibonacci(100)
// Fibonacci(500)
// 堆栈溢出了
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果我们使用尾递归优化过的fibonacci 递归算法</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function Fibonacci2 (n , ac1 = 1 , ac2 = 1) {
  if( n &lt;= 1 ) {return ac2};

  return Fibonacci2 (n - 1, ac2, ac1 + ac2);
}

Fibonacci2(100) // 573147844013817200000
Fibonacci2(1000) // 7.0330367711422765e+208
Fibonacci2(10000) // Infinity
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">由此可见，“尾调用优化”对递归操作意义重大，所以一些函数式编程语言将其写入了语言规格。ES6也是如此，第一次明确规定，所有ECMAScript的实现，都必须部署“尾调用优化”。这就是说，在ES6中，只要使用尾递归，就不会发生栈溢出，相对节省内存。</p><h3 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">递归函数的改写</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">尾递归的实现，往往需要改写递归函数，确保最后一步只调用自身。做到这一点的方法，就是把所有用到的内部变量改写成函数的参数。比如上面的例子，阶乘函数 factorial 需要用到一个中间变量 total ，那就把这个中间变量改写成函数的参数。这样做的缺点就是不太直观，第一眼很难看出来，为什么计算5的阶乘，需要传入两个参数5和1？</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">两个方法可以解决这个问题。方法一是在尾递归函数之外，再提供一个正常形式的函数。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function tailFactorial(n, total) {
  if (n === 1) return total;
  return tailFactorial(n - 1, n * total);
}

function factorial(n) {
  return tailFactorial(n, 1);
}

factorial(5) // 120
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码通过一个正常形式的阶乘函数 factorial ，调用尾递归函数 tailFactorial ，看起来就正常多了。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">函数式编程有一个概念，叫做柯里化（currying），意思是将多参数的函数转换成单参数的形式。这里也可以使用柯里化。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function currying(fn, n) {
  return function (m) {
    return fn.call(this, m, n);
  };
}

function tailFactorial(n, total) {
  if (n === 1) return total;
  return tailFactorial(n - 1, n * total);
}

const factorial = currying(tailFactorial, 1);

factorial(5) // 120
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码通过柯里化，将尾递归函数 tailFactorial 变为只接受1个参数的 factorial 。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">第二种方法就简单多了，就是采用ES6的函数默认值。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function factorial(n, total = 1) {
  if (n === 1) return total;
  return factorial(n - 1, n * total);
}

factorial(5) // 120
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，参数 total 有默认值1，所以调用时不用提供这个值。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">总结一下，递归本质上是一种循环操作。纯粹的函数式编程语言没有循环操作命令，所有的循环都用递归实现，这就是为什么尾递归对这些语言极其重要。对于其他支持“尾调用优化”的语言（比如Lua，ES6），只需要知道循环可以用递归代替，而一旦使用递归，就最好使用尾递归。</p><h3 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">严格模式</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">ES6的尾调用优化只在严格模式下开启，正常模式是无效的。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">这是因为在正常模式下，函数内部有两个变量，可以跟踪函数的调用栈。</p><ul style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 2em; list-style: none; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">func.arguments</code>：返回调用时函数的参数。</li><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0.25em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">func.caller</code>：返回调用当前函数的那个函数。</li></ul><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">尾调用优化发生时，函数的调用栈会改写，因此上面两个变量就会失真。严格模式禁用这两个变量，所以尾调用模式仅在严格模式下生效。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function restricted() {
  "use strict";
  restricted.caller;    // 报错
  restricted.arguments; // 报错
}
restricted();
</code></pre><h3 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">尾递归优化的实现</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">尾递归优化只在严格模式下生效，那么正常模式下，或者那些不支持该功能的环境中，有没有办法也使用尾递归优化呢？回答是可以的，就是自己实现尾递归优化。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">它的原理非常简单。尾递归之所以需要优化，原因是调用栈太多，造成溢出，那么只要减少调用栈，就不会溢出。怎么做可以减少调用栈呢？就是采用“循环”换掉“递归”。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">下面是一个正常的递归函数。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function sum(x, y) {
  if (y &gt; 0) {
    return sum(x + 1, y - 1);
  } else {
    return x;
  }
}

sum(1, 100000)
// Uncaught RangeError: Maximum call stack size exceeded(…)
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">sum</code>是一个递归函数，参数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">x</code>是需要累加的值，参数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">y</code>控制递归次数。一旦指定<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">sum</code>递归100000次，就会报错，提示超出调用栈的最大次数。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">蹦床函数（trampoline）可以将递归执行转为循环执行。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function trampoline(f) {
  while (f &amp;&amp; f instanceof Function) {
    f = f();
  }
  return f;
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面就是蹦床函数的一个实现，它接受一个函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">f</code>作为参数。只要<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">f</code>执行后返回一个函数，就继续执行。注意，这里是返回一个函数，然后执行该函数，而不是函数里面调用函数，这样就避免了递归执行，从而就消除了调用栈过大的问题。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">然后，要做的就是将原来的递归函数，改写为每一步返回另一个函数。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function sum(x, y) {
  if (y &gt; 0) {
    return sum.bind(null, x + 1, y - 1);
  } else {
    return x;
  }
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">sum</code>函数的每次执行，都会返回自身的另一个版本。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">现在，使用蹦床函数执行<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">sum</code>，就不会发生调用栈溢出。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">trampoline(sum(1, 100000))
// 100001
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">蹦床函数并不是真正的尾递归优化，下面的实现才是。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function tco(f) {
  var value;
  var active = false;
  var accumulated = [];

  return function accumulator() {
    accumulated.push(arguments);
    if (!active) {
      active = true;
      while (accumulated.length) {
        value = f.apply(this, accumulated.shift());
      }
      active = false;
      return value;
    }
  };
}

var sum = tco(function(x, y) {
  if (y &gt; 0) {
    return sum(x + 1, y - 1)
  }
  else {
    return x
  }
});

sum(1, 100000)
// 100001
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">tco</code>函数是尾递归优化的实现，它的奥妙就在于状态变量<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">active</code>。默认情况下，这个变量是不激活的。一旦进入尾递归优化的过程，这个变量就激活了。然后，每一轮递归<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">sum</code>返回的都是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">undefined</code>，所以就避免了递归执行；而<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">accumulated</code>数组存放每一轮<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">sum</code>执行的参数，总是有值的，这就保证了<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">accumulator</code>函数内部的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">while</code>循环总是会执行。这样就很巧妙地将“递归”改成了“循环”，而后一轮的参数会取代前一轮的参数，保证了调用栈只有一层。</p><h2 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px 0px 0.3em; top: -900em; left: -900em; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">函数参数的尾逗号</h2><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">ES2017<span class="Apple-converted-space">&nbsp;</span><a href="https://github.com/jeffmo/es-trailing-function-commas" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; outline: 0px; color: rgb(64, 120, 192); text-decoration-line: none; box-sizing: border-box; background-color: transparent;">允许</a>函数的最后一个参数有尾逗号（trailing comma）。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">此前，函数定义和调用时，都不允许最后一个参数后面出现逗号。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function clownsEverywhere(
  param1,
  param2
) { /* ... */ }

clownsEverywhere(
  'foo',
  'bar'
);
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，如果在<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">param2</code>或<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">bar</code>后面加一个逗号，就会报错。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果像上面这样，将参数写成多行（即每个参数占据一行），以后修改代码的时候，想为函数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">clownsEverywhere</code>添加第三个参数，或者调整参数的次序，就势必要在原来最后一个参数后面添加一个逗号。这对于版本管理系统来说，就会显示添加逗号的那一行也发生了变动。这看上去有点冗余，因此新的语法允许定义和调用时，尾部直接有一个逗号。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function clownsEverywhere(
  param1,
  param2,
) { /* ... */ }

clownsEverywhere(
  'foo',
  'bar',
);
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-left: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;; margin-bottom: 0px !important;">这样的规定也使得，函数参数与数组和对象的尾逗号规则，保持一致了。</p></div>
